import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}
```---

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */

    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]

    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher

    public void testCharMatcher() {

        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");

        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");

    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;

import java.util.List;

 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]

        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();

        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */

    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白

                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格

        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}
```---

title: Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09

     */

        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}
```---

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09

     */
    @Test

        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");

        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串

                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]

     */

        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");

        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");

                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */

        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");

        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");

        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */

    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');

        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;

import java.util.List;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */

        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */

                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白

                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格

        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**

     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");

        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}
```---

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');

        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**

     */

    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}
```---

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;

import java.util.List;

 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09

     */

        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");

        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher

        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格

        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");

    /**

    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");

                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白

                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09

     */

        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */

        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");

        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}
```---
date: 2022-04-27T02:21:37+08:00

title: Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */

    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');

        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");

        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name

        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */
public class StringTestClient {

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher

        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */
    @Test
    public void testSplitter() {
        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白
                .omitEmptyStrings()//从结果中自动忽略空字符串
                .splitToList("foo;bar;;  ; qux;");
        assertThat(list1).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("foo", "bar", "qux"));

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
        assertThat(spaced).isEqualTo("一个 CharMatcher 代表 一类 字符");

        //用*号替换所有数字
        String noDigits = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.replaceFrom("我的手机号是13400001234", "*");
        assertThat(noDigits).isEqualTo("我的手机号是***********");

        // 只保留数字和小写字母
        String lowerAndDigit = CharMatcher.JAVA_DIGIT.or(CharMatcher.JAVA_LOWER_CASE).retainFrom("yutianran1314@gmail.COM");
        assertThat(lowerAndDigit).isEqualTo("yutianran1314gmail");


    }

    /**
     * 测试变量格式器-CaseFormat
     */
    @Test
    public void testCaseFormat() {
        //userName -> user-name
        String lowerHyphen = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_HYPHEN, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerHyphen).isEqualTo("user-name");

        //userName -> user_name
        String lowerUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.LOWER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(lowerUnderscore).isEqualTo("user_name");

        //userName -> UserName
        String upperCamel = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_CAMEL, "userName");
        assertThat(upperCamel).isEqualTo("UserName");

        //userName -> USER_NAME
        String upperUnderscore = CaseFormat.LOWER_CAMEL.to(CaseFormat.UPPER_UNDERSCORE, "userName");
        assertThat(upperUnderscore).isEqualTo("USER_NAME");
    }
}

# Guava字符串处理：连接，拆分，匹配，格式

>这里，Guava将常用的字符串处理设计了4种角色：连接器、拆分器、匹配器、格式器，很方便我们自己拓展，强大！

感觉Guava采用的Fluent风格还是不错的，和RxJava的使用有点像，链式调用，阅读性很好，可以好好学习下。

---
废话少说了，上代码：

```
package com.che.baseutil.guava.string;

import com.google.common.base.CaseFormat;
import com.google.common.base.CharMatcher;
import com.google.common.base.Joiner;
import com.google.common.base.Splitter;
import com.google.common.collect.Lists;

import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;

import static com.google.common.truth.Truth.assertThat;

/**
 * Guava字符串处理：分割，连接，匹配，格式
 *
 * @gradle testCompile 'com.google.truth:truth:0.27' [794]
 * @gradle compile 'com.google.guava:guava:19.0' [15076]
 * 作者：余天然 on 16/9/16 上午11:09
 */

    /**
     * 测试连接器-Joiner
     */
    @Test
    public void testJoiner() {
        Joiner joiner = Joiner.on(";").skipNulls();
        String result1 = joiner.join("Harry", null, "Ron", "Hermione");
        assertThat(result1).isEqualTo("Harry;Ron;Hermione");

        String result2 = Joiner.on(",").join(Arrays.asList(1, 5, 7));
        assertThat(result2).isEqualTo("1,5,7");
    }

    /**
     * 测试拆分器-Splitter
     */

        List<String> list1 = Splitter.on(';')
                .trimResults()//移除结果字符串的前导空白和尾部空白

        List<String> list2 = Splitter.fixedLength(3)//限制拆分出的字符串数量
                .splitToList("这使得splitter实例都是线程安全的");
        assertThat(list2).isEqualTo(Lists.newArrayList("这使得", "spl", "itt", "er实", "例都是", "线程安", "全的"));
    }

    /**
     * 测试字符匹配器-CharMatcher
     */
    @Test
    public void testCharMatcher() {
        //只保留数字字符
        String theDigits = CharMatcher.DIGIT.retainFrom("今天是2016年9月16日");
        assertThat(theDigits).isEqualTo("2016916");

        //去除两端的空格，并把中间的连续空格替换成单个空格
        String spaced = CharMatcher.WHITESPACE.trimAndCollapseFrom("  一个 CharMatcher   代表 一类 字符 ", ' ');
